<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;
text-align:right;line-height:normal;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:
none'>&nbsp;</p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;
text-align:right;line-height:normal;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:
none'>&nbsp;</p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;
text-align:right;line-height:normal;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:
none'><b><font size="2">EXHIBIT
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>
<img border="0" src="ffmlogo.jpg" width="384" height="164"></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:325.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:right;
punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><b><font size="2">For
additional information contact <br>
Bobby Krimmel <br>
Chief Financial Officer <br>
(931)
380-8257</font></b></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-right:2.0pt;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:1.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:7.9pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none' align="center"><b>FIRST FARMERS AND
MERCHANTS CORPORATION REPORTS SECOND QUARTER NET INCOME OF $2.7 MILLION, OR
$0.56 PER COMMON SHARE</b></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;
text-autospace:none'><font size="2">COLUMBIA, Tenn. (July 23, 2015) &#150;First Farmers and
Merchants Corporation, (&#147;First Farmers&#148;), the holding company for First Farmers
and Merchants Bank (&#147;the Bank&#148;), today announced unaudited financial results
for the quarter ending June 30, 2015, showing increases in earnings, loan
growth, and net interest income.</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Key
highlights of First Farmers&#146;results for the second quarter of 2015 include:</font></p>

<ul>
	<li>
	<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Net income of
$2.7 million or $0.56 per common share, up 3% from $2.6 million or $0.53 per
common share for the previous quarter, and up 4% from $2.6 million or $0.52 per
common share for the year-earlier quarter; </font></p></li>
	<li>
	<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Loan growth of
$10 million or 2% from the previous quarter and $67 million or 11% compared
with the year-earlier quarter; </font></p></li>
	<li>
	<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;
punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Deposit growth of
$90 million or 9% compared with the year-earlier quarter; and </font></p></li>
	<li>
	<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;
punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">A decline in
nonperforming assets of $2.7 million or 52% compared with the previous quarter
and $8.9 million or 78% compared with the year-earlier quarter. </font></p></li>
</ul>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-right:8.0pt;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;
text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Commenting on the results, T. Randy Stevens,
Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of First Farmers, said &#147;We are pleased to
report another solid quarter of earnings per share growth, while at the same
time reporting credit quality metrics which demonstrate further improvements in
portfolio risks.&#148; Stevens added, &#147;Our continued strategy of expansion into the Williamson
and Davidson County markets, while continuing to serve our traditional markets
at the highest level, and the hiring of high quality bankers has allowed us to
record double-digit year-over-year loan growth.&#148;</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:8pt;line-height:
normal;text-autospace:none'><b><font size="2">Second
Quarter 2015 Results of Operations</font></b></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:35.05pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">The $85,000 increase in
reported quarterly earnings for the second quarter of 2015 compared with the
previous quarter was primarily driven by increased loan volume. The $105,000
increase in reported quarterly earnings for the second quarter of 2015 compared
with the year-earlier quarter was primarily driven by increased loan volume and
improvement in the corporation&#146;s effective tax rate for income taxes.</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:35.05pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">For the second quarter
of 2015, First Farmers continued to achieve solid loan growth of $10 million or
2% from the previous quarter and advancing $67 million or 11% compared with the
year-earlier quarter, driven primarily by increased commercial and residential
mortgage lending. While down 1% from the previous quarter, total deposits
increased 9% from the year-earlier quarter from $967 million to $1.057 billion.</font></p>

</div>

&nbsp;<div style='page:WordSection2;'>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;text-autospace:none' align="center"><b><font size="2">-MORE-</font></b></p>

</div>

<font face="Arial" size="2">

<hr>

<p style='page-break-before:always'></p>


</font>


<div style='page:WordSection3;'>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;text-autospace:none'>
<font size="2">FFMH Reports Second Quarter
2015 Results</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">July 23, 2015</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Page 2</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;text-autospace:none'><b><font size="2">Asset Quality</font></b></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-right:8.0pt;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:35.05pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Total
nonperforming assets decreased to $2.5 million, or 0.21% of total assets,
compared to $5.2 million, or 0.43% of total assets, for the previous quarter
and declined from $11.4 million, or 1.02% of total assets, compared to the
year-earlier quarter. Net recoveries to average loans were 0.19% for the second
quarter of 2015 compared to 0.01% for the previous quarter and 0.01% for the
year-earlier quarter. As a result of continued improvement in credit trends, no
provision to the allowance for loan losses was recorded during the second
quarter of 2015, which represented 1.25% of total loans outstanding as of June
30, 2015 versus 1.18% for the previous quarter and 1.40% for year-earlier
quarter.</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;text-autospace:none'><b><font size="2">About First Farmers and Merchants Corporation and First Farmers
and Merchants Bank</font></b></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-top:0in;margin-right:5.0pt;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;
text-indent:35.05pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:
none'><font size="2">First Farmers and Merchants Corporation is the holding company for
First Farmers and Merchants Bank, a community bank serving the Middle Tennessee
area through 19 banking locations in eight Middle Tennessee counties. As of
June 30, 2015, First Farmers reported total assets of approximately $1.2
billion and total shareholders&#146;equity of approximately $116 million. For more information about
First Farmers, visit First Farmers and Merchants Bank on the Web at <u>www.myfirstfarmers.com</u> under
the &quot;Our Story&quot; and &quot;Investor Relations&quot; tab.</font></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:115%;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;text-autospace:none'><b><font size="2">Cautionary
Note Regarding Forward Looking Statements</font></b></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-family:"Arial";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:
justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:35.05pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none'><font size="2">Except for historical
information contained herein, the matters included in this news release and
other information in First Farmers&#146;filings with the Securities and Exchange
Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;) may contain certain &quot;forward-looking
statements,&quot; within the meaning of Section 27A of the Securities Act of
1933, as amended, and Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as
amended. These statements can be identified by the fact that they do not relate
strictly to historical or current facts and often use words or phrases such as
&quot;opportunities,&quot; &quot;prospects,&quot; &quot;will likely
result,&quot; &quot;are expected to,&quot; &quot;will continue,&quot; &quot;is

&quot;intends&quot; or similar expressions. The forward-looking statements

</font>


<div style='page:WordSection4;'>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0in;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-autospace:none'>&nbsp;</p>
